            preloadBannerSdk();

            ONE_TRUST_LIBRARIES.forEach((library) => {
                loadScript(library.url, "text/javascript", library.options);
            });

            if (country === "US") {
                loadCCPAAddon();
            }
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithOneTrustEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithOneTrustEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            script.setAttribute("data-domain-script", DATA_DOMAIN_SCRIPT);

            return script;
        }

        function loadCCPAAddon() {
            loadScript(CCPA_ADDON.url, "text/javascript", CCPA_ADDON.options);
        }

        function preloadBannerSdk() {
            const link = document.createElement("link");
            link.href = BANNER_SDK.url;
            link.rel = "preload";
            link.as = "script";

            document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        function oneTrustLoaded() {
            return !!(window.OneTrust || window.OneTrustStub);
        }

        console.debug('OneTrust setup', countriesWithOneTrustEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !oneTrustLoaded()) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!oneTrustLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            const countriesWithKetchEnabled = {"countries":["IN","HU","SG"]};
            if (!countriesWithKetchEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithKetchEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithKetchEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }


        function loadKetchScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            if (!shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            window.semaphore = window.semaphore || [];

            window.ketch = function () {
                window.semaphore.push(arguments);
            };

            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
            var property = urlParams.has("property") ? urlParams.get("property") : "website_smart_tag";

            var scriptElement = document.createElement("script");
            scriptElement.type = "text/javascript";
            scriptElement.src = "https://global.ketchcdn.com/web/v2/config/fandom/" + property + "/boot.js";
            scriptElement.defer = scriptElement.async = true;

            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(scriptElement);
        }

        function ketchLoaded() {
            return !!window.ketch;
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !ketchLoaded()) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!ketchLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (async function () {
        // const AIRGAP_URL = '<script
        // data-cfasync="false"
        // src=""
        const AIRGAP_URL = 'https://transcend-cdn.com/cm/54b0c313-5d22-47e5-92fd-f979a37d1ad0/airgap.js';
        const countriesWithAirgapEnabled = [];

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {

            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadAirgapScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            const enabled = shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) || airgapScriptForced();

            if (!enabled) {
                return;
            }

            loadScript(AIRGAP_URL, "text/javascript", {
                'data-cfasync': false
            });
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithAirgapEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function airgapScriptForced() {
            return window.location.search.includes('icPreferredCMP=airgap');
        }

        function shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithAirgapEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithAirgapEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            return script;
        }

        console.debug('Airgap setup', countriesWithAirgapEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        let geo = getGeo();

        if (geo === null) {
            geo = await waitForGeo();
        }

        if (geo) {
            loadAirgapScripts(geo);
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean(false);

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;
	}

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {
		document.documentElement.classList.add('is-content-expanded');
	}
</script>

													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"sXWp3rZ0","connatixPlaylistId":"36081eca-e784-4e30-87c3-133cf673e447","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["AE","AG","AL","AM","AR","AT","AU","AZ","BA","BB","BD","BG","BH","BN","BO","BR","BS","BY","CA","CH","CL","CN","CO","CR","CU","CY","CZ","DE","DK","DO","DZ","EC","EE","EG","ES","FI","FR","GB","GE","GF","GG","GH","GP","GR","GT","GU","GY","HK","HN","HR","HU","ID","IE","IL","IM","IN","IQ","IR","IS","IT","JE","JM","JO","JP","KE","KG","KH","KR","KW","KY","KZ","LA","LB","LK","LT","LU","LV","LY","MA","MD","ME","MK","MM","MN","MO","MQ","MT","MU","MV","MX","MY","NG","NI","NO","NP","NZ","OM","PA","PE","PH","PK","PL","PR","PS","PT","PY","QA","RE","RO","RS","RU","SA","SC","SE","SG","SI","SK","SV","TD","TH","TN","TR","TT","TW","UA","US","UY","UZ","VE","VI","VN","ZA","ZW"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT","PE","CO","CL","NZ"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.fandomIsVideoPossible = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping &&
					isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() &&
					!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			return window.fandomIsVideoPossible()
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

<dl><dd><span class="dablink"><i>For the newspaper reporter and Underworld emperor, see <a href="/wiki/Morgans" title="Morgans">Morgans</a>.</i></span></dd></dl>
<p><b>"Axe-Hand" Morgan</b><sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_4-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> is a former <a href="/wiki/Marine" class="mw-redirect" title="Marine">Marine</a> <a href="/wiki/Captain_(Marine_Rank)" title="Captain (Marine Rank)">captain</a>, the father of <a href="/wiki/Helmeppo" title="Helmeppo">Helmeppo</a> and the first significant Marine officer to appear in the storyline.<sup id="cite_ref-intro_1-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> After his defeat by <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> and <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a>, he was stripped of his rank for his many abuses of power.
</p><p>He is the third antagonist of the <a href="/wiki/Romance_Dawn_Arc" title="Romance Dawn Arc">Romance Dawn Arc</a>, serving as the main antagonist of the <a href="/wiki/Shells_Town" title="Shells Town">Shells Town</a> subsection. He is also the main antagonist of the <a href="/wiki/Diary_of_Koby-Meppo" title="Diary of Koby-Meppo">Diary of Koby-Meppo</a> cover-page serial.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance">Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Morgan is a notably towering, muscular man with tanned skin, blonde hair, a well-defined face, and a steel jaw etched with the word <i><b>Möwe</b></i> (German for "seagull").<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> As his <a href="/wiki/Epithet" title="Epithet">epithet</a> suggests, his right hand has been replaced with a huge steel axe, the handle of which is not only bolted through the bones of his forearm, but sticks out where his elbow should be.
</p><p>Like most Marine officers, he wears a large, ornate overcoat. However, this coat notably lacks the usual "Justice"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">正義</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> insignia, and is completely sleeveless; it is also worn conventionally, instead of being draped over the shoulders like a cape. His trousers bear a striped pattern reminiscent of <a href="/wiki/Marine_Base" title="Marine Base">Marine Bases</a> and <a href="/wiki/Marine_Ships" title="Marine Ships">battleships</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-intro_1-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In peacetime, he can often be seen smoking a cigar.
</p><p>As a no-name Marine, Morgan had a cleft chin similar to his son’s (though this apparently developed after his youth), and his arms were both whole and a little less muscular, though he still seemed very well-built. During the attack by <a href="/wiki/Kuro" title="Kuro">Captain Kuro</a>, his arm was maimed and his chin shattered, necessitating his future prosthetics. He wore a standard Marine uniform, which was slashed across the front by Kuro’s signature <a href="/wiki/Cat_Claws" title="Cat Claws">Cat Claws</a>.
</p><p>After his defeat and arrest, Morgan was put into a standard striped prisoner's uniform, and shackled around the arms and legs.<sup id="cite_ref-c88_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c88-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> While he eventually rid himself of the shackles, the prisoner's uniform has remained his last known outfit to date.<sup id="cite_ref-c132_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c132-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

</div></span></div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D4&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">Rank means <b>everything</b> in this world, remember that! My rank is the highest on this base... which makes me superior to everyone else here... <b>That means everything I do is right!</b></td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:&#39;Arial&#39;,sans-serif;">—&#160;Morgan.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p>In his youth, Morgan was a brave, tenacious Marine, willing to defy enemies even on the brink of death.<sup id="cite_ref-c37_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c37-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> In time, however, his success corrupted him until he became a brutal tyrant obsessed with his personal status and glory above all.<sup id="cite_ref-obsession_with_rank_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-obsession_with_rank-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As such, Morgan's usual demeanor is similar to that of many <a href="/wiki/Pirate" title="Pirate">pirates</a>: ruling chiefly through terror, quick to threaten execution for the slightest defiance, and utterly convinced of his own infallibility.<sup id="cite_ref-terror_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-terror-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> Such is his narcissism that he considered a statue of himself (funded by taxes coerced from <a href="/wiki/Shells_Town" title="Shells Town">Shells Town</a>'s citizens) one of his greatest accomplishments.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Following his defeat and arrest, Morgan also displayed enough cunning to successfully escape custody. Family loyalty meant nothing to him, as he callously took his son as hostage despite the boy was, at the time, the sole person who still cared for him. What motives or goals he may have adopted since are unknown. However, he became lax enough to take a nap while sailing away.<sup id="cite_ref-c132_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c132-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D5&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Family">Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Helmeppo">Helmeppo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Morgan's main relation is his son <a href="/wiki/Helmeppo" title="Helmeppo">Helmeppo</a>. At the height of his career, he let Helmeppo act as a sort of unofficial deputy, bullying local civilians (and even subordinate Marines) under Morgan's own authority.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> While Helmeppo thought this stemmed from fatherly love, Morgan never truly possessed any, and casually answered Helmeppo's complaint about being struck by <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> with a blow of his own, adding that his son had simply not been "worth" hitting before.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>This (along with seeing Morgan's willingness to kill even <a href="/wiki/Rika" title="Rika">children</a>) deeply unsettled Helmeppo's views of his father. However, their relationship did not completely collapse until some time after Morgan's defeat and imprisonment.<sup id="cite_ref-c89_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c89-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> Uncaring that Helmeppo alone was genuinely concerned for his fate, Morgan took the boy hostage to escape custody, spurring Helmeppo to disown him and flee at the first opportunity.<sup id="cite_ref-c95_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c95-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c102_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c102-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Crew">Crew</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>What relationship Morgan initially had with his fellow Marines is unknown. Once he became commander of the <a href="/wiki/153rd_Branch" title="153rd Branch">153rd Branch</a>, however, he tyrannized his subordinates as mercilessly as he did civilians, forcing them to collect heavy taxes and arrest—if not outright kill—anyone who displeased him. Those who disobeyed for any reason were inevitably executed as "traitors" by Morgan himself.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Due to this, the rest of the 153rd unanimously hated Morgan, rejoicing in his defeat and quickly imprisoning him afterward.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In his youth, Morgan was the sole survivor of an attack by <a href="/wiki/Kuro" title="Kuro">Captain Kuro</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Black_Cat_Pirates" title="Black Cat Pirates">Black Cat Pirates</a>, and was subsequently <a href="/wiki/Jango#Abilities_and_Powers" title="Jango">hypnotized</a> into thinking he had captured the infamous pirate. Neither man is known to have thought about the other since, though Morgan continues to allude to the incident as justification for his Captain rank.<sup id="cite_ref-obsession_with_rank_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-obsession_with_rank-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Morgan's most prominent enemies are, of course, the inaugural members of the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a>—<a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> and <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a>. While condemning both for defying his rule, Morgan did not judge either a significant threat, claiming Zoro's strength was "dust" compared to his own and refusing to give in even after Luffy effortlessly outfought him.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> It is unknown whether he ever changed these judgments after his defeat.
</p><p>Apart from the Straw Hats, Morgan also served as an important foe for <a href="/wiki/Koby" title="Koby">Koby</a>, tempering his dream to join the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a> with a realization that they could be as corruptible and fallible as any men.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Even as a recruit, Morgan was notably tougher than average, surviving an onslaught from <a href="/wiki/Kuro" title="Kuro">Captain Kuro</a> that instantly killed dozens of other Marines (though it should be noted that not finishing him was a deliberate choice on Kuro's part).<sup id="cite_ref-c37_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c37-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As Captain of the 153rd, Morgan possessed notably more muscle and bulk, enough to easily lift an average-sized man by the neck, as well as complete authority over an entire base of Marine swordsmen and riflemen.<sup id="cite_ref-terror_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-terror-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> While he lost this authority after his arrest, he still maintained enough strength to burst a set of metal shackles from the inside-out.<sup id="cite_ref-c95_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c95-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He also possesses some knowledge of <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruits</a> despite their rarity in the <a href="/wiki/East_Blue" title="East Blue">East Blue</a>, immediately identifying them as the source of <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi">rubber body</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Weapons">Weapons</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Morgan's axe-hand is a completely functional weapon, sharp and sturdy enough to bisect an entire chain-link fence and create small fissures in the ground.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Despite its unwieldy appearance, Morgan is able to maneuver it with ease.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Past">Past</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/ff/Kuro_Breaks_Morgan%27s_Jaw.png/revision/latest?cb=20230319223453" class="image"><img alt="Kuro Breaks Morgan&#39;s Jaw" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kuro Breaks Morgan&#39;s Jaw.png" data-image-key="Kuro_Breaks_Morgan%27s_Jaw.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/ff/Kuro_Breaks_Morgan%27s_Jaw.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230319223453" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/ff/Kuro_Breaks_Morgan%27s_Jaw.png/revision/latest?cb=20230319223453" class="image"><img alt="Kuro Breaks Morgan&#39;s Jaw" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/ff/Kuro_Breaks_Morgan%27s_Jaw.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230319223453" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kuro Breaks Morgan&#39;s Jaw.png" data-image-key="Kuro_Breaks_Morgan%27s_Jaw.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/ff/Kuro_Breaks_Morgan%27s_Jaw.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230319223453" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kuro_Breaks_Morgan%27s_Jaw.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuro defeats Morgan.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Twenty two years ago, Morgan fathered a son named <a href="/wiki/Helmeppo" title="Helmeppo">Helmeppo</a> and led a largely unremarkable life in the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>. Until an event that occurred 3 years before the the start of the story, on the fateful night his crew attacked the <a href="/wiki/Black_Cat_Pirates" title="Black Cat Pirates">Black Cat Pirates</a>, incurring the wrath of the infamous <a href="/wiki/Kuro" title="Kuro">Captain Kuro</a>. With his superhuman speed and <a href="/wiki/Cat_Claws" title="Cat Claws">deadly claws</a>, Kuro easily massacred all of Morgan's crewmates, leaving Morgan himself just barely alive with a broken jaw and a maimed arm. The defiant Morgan refused to beg for his life, but was spared anyway, as Kuro had long schemed to retire from piracy undisturbed; Morgan, deemed an ideal pawn for this scheme, was hypnotized by <a href="/wiki/Jango" title="Jango">Jango</a> into believing that he had captured Kuro, and sent off with <a href="/wiki/Nugire_Yainu" title="Nugire Yainu">a lookalike pirate</a> (hypnotized into believing that he was Kuro).<sup id="cite_ref-c37_10-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c37-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After "Kuro" was executed, Morgan—a mere chief petty officer at the time—was given sole credit for the capture and quickly promoted to <a href="/wiki/Lieutenant_commander" class="mw-redirect" title="Lieutenant commander">lieutenant commander</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-SBS6_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SBS6-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Within the next three years, his obsession with rank and power carried him even higher, until he was appointed captain of the <a href="/wiki/153rd_Branch" title="153rd Branch">153rd Branch</a> and given absolute authority over the surrounding community of <a href="/wiki/Shells_Town" title="Shells Town">Shells Town</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-obsession_with_rank_11-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-obsession_with_rank-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="East_Blue_Saga">East Blue Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Romance_Dawn_Arc">Romance Dawn Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>By the time <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a> arrived at Shells Town, Morgan had become an outright tyrant, extracting high taxes from the townsfolk (who grew to fear the mere mention of his name) and building monuments to himself. None dared challenge his rule, as he had no qualms about killing "traitors", up to and including his own men. His son <a href="/wiki/Helmeppo" title="Helmeppo">Helmeppo</a> regularly exploited this, forcing the townsfolk to grovel and cater to his every whim; when Zoro refused to follow suit, even killing <a href="/wiki/Soro" title="Soro">Helmeppo's pet wolf</a> for threatening a local girl named <a href="/wiki/Rika" title="Rika">Rika</a>, Morgan indulged his son's request to have the bounty hunter arrested and starved for a month.
</p><p>However, after nine days of starvation failed to break Zoro, Morgan and Helmeppo decided to execute the bounty hunter as a warning to the townsfolk. Around the same time, reports of the arrest led rookie pirate <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> and aspiring Marine <a href="/wiki/Koby" title="Koby">Koby</a> to Shells Town, partly in hopes of recruiting Zoro. Upon arriving, the pair condemned Morgan's rule and resolved to free Zoro, and Luffy outright attacked Helmeppo after overhearing the execution plans. At first, Morgan cared little about these newcomers, even striking Helmeppo himself when urged to punish them; his wrath was instead focused on Rika, who had been caught smuggling food to Zoro that same day. To the horror of the entire base (including Helmeppo), Morgan ordered the girl executed, and immediately maimed <a href="/wiki/Rokkaku" title="Rokkaku">his closest lieutenant</a> for protesting.
</p><p>All the while, Morgan remained unaware that Luffy had begun searching the base for Zoro's confiscated swords until Luffy forced his way onto the roof, unwittingly breaking a just-finished statue of Morgan.<sup id="cite_ref-intro_1-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> Seconds later, Koby was caught trying to free Zoro, and a furious Morgan deployed his entire troop with orders to kill, only for Luffy and Zoro to easily beat them all.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/db/Luffy_vs._Morgan.png/revision/latest?cb=20230209162718" class="image"><img alt="Luffy vs" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Luffy vs. Morgan.png" data-image-key="Luffy_vs._Morgan.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/db/Luffy_vs._Morgan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230209162718" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/db/Luffy_vs._Morgan.png/revision/latest?cb=20230209162718" class="image"><img alt="Luffy vs" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/db/Luffy_vs._Morgan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230209162718" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Luffy vs. Morgan.png" data-image-key="Luffy_vs._Morgan.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/db/Luffy_vs._Morgan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230209162718" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Luffy_vs._Morgan.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">His subordinates beaten, Morgan prepares to fight Luffy and Zoro himself.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Unsympathetic, Morgan ordered all of the "defeatists" to commit suicide, and tried to fight Luffy one-on-one, but found his great strength useless against the younger, faster pirate. Though the one-sided battle was interrupted by Helmeppo (who took Koby hostage with a <a href="/wiki/Firearm" title="Firearm">pistol</a>), Morgan was cut down by Zoro before he could press the advantage.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On seeing their captain defeated, Morgan's men immediately began celebrating, overjoyed to be free of his tyranny. Subsequently, Morgan was detained in the very base he once commanded, while <a href="/wiki/Ripper" title="Ripper">one of his former lieutenants</a> took charge of the 153rd Branch.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>The following events are <a href="/wiki/Canon#Non-Canon" title="Canon">Non-Canon</a> and therefore not considered part of the <a href="/wiki/Canon" title="Canon">Canon</a> story.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Loguetown_Arc">Loguetown Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>News of Luffy's <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>30,000,000 bounty was personally delivered to the incarcerated Morgan by one of his cell guards, and left him newly furious.<sup id="cite_ref-ep45_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ep45-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
<small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>Concludes non-canon section.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Diary_of_Koby-Meppo">Diary of Koby-Meppo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a6/Morgan%27s_Escape.png/revision/latest?cb=20230722024258" class="image"><img alt="Morgan&#39;s Escape" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Morgan&#39;s Escape.png" data-image-key="Morgan%27s_Escape.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a6/Morgan%27s_Escape.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230722024258" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a6/Morgan%27s_Escape.png/revision/latest?cb=20230722024258" class="image"><img alt="Morgan&#39;s Escape" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a6/Morgan%27s_Escape.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230722024258" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Morgan&#39;s Escape.png" data-image-key="Morgan%27s_Escape.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a6/Morgan%27s_Escape.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230722024258" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Morgan%27s_Escape.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Morgan escapes, holding Helmeppo hostage.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Eventually, Morgan was formally arraigned for his crimes by <a href="/wiki/Marine_Headquarters" title="Marine Headquarters">Marine Headquarters</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c88_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c88-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> His impending court-martial became a subject of much discussion among the 153rd Branch—particularly the newly-enlisted Koby and Helmeppo, who now viewed him with a mixture of fear and compunction.<sup id="cite_ref-c89_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c89-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On the day of the court-martial, Morgan was transferred to an escort ship captained by the renowned <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Vice-Admiral Garp</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> In mid-transfer, however, Garp fell into one of his irregular sleeping fits, and Morgan immediately seized the opening to attack the Vice-Admiral<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> before taking Helmeppo hostage.<sup id="cite_ref-c95_17-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c95-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> This allowed Morgan to successfully escape in a lifeboat,<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> but destroyed the last of his relationship with his son, who openly disowned him and swam back to Garp's ship.<sup id="cite_ref-c102_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c102-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>For his part, Morgan made no effort to pursue his son, and continued along the open sea by himself.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Arabasta_Saga">Arabasta Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="Jango.27s_Dance_Paradise"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Jango's_Dance_Paradise">Jango's Dance Paradise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fc/Morgan_Passes_Jango.png/revision/latest?cb=20140916073331" class="image"><img alt="Morgan Passes Jango" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="207" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Morgan Passes Jango.png" data-image-key="Morgan_Passes_Jango.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fc/Morgan_Passes_Jango.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20140916073331" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fc/Morgan_Passes_Jango.png/revision/latest?cb=20140916073331" class="image"><img alt="Morgan Passes Jango" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fc/Morgan_Passes_Jango.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20140916073331" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="207" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Morgan Passes Jango.png" data-image-key="Morgan_Passes_Jango.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fc/Morgan_Passes_Jango.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20140916073331" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Morgan_Passes_Jango.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Morgan is seen passing <a href="/wiki/Jango" title="Jango">Jango</a> after his escape.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>By the time of <a href="/wiki/Jango" title="Jango">Jango</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Jango%27s_Dance_Paradise" title="Jango&#39;s Dance Paradise">flight</a> from <a href="/wiki/Syrup_Village" title="Syrup Village">Syrup Village</a>, Morgan remained at large. The two men, both napping, passed one another without ever realizing it.<sup id="cite_ref-c132_8-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c132-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>What became of Morgan since—and whether any Marines are still in active pursuit of him—is unknown.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Major_Battles">Major Battles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Morgan vs. <a href="/wiki/Kuro" title="Kuro">Kuro</a></li>
<li>Morgan vs. <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> and <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a></li>
<li>Morgan vs. <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Monkey D. Garp</a></li>
<li>Morgan vs. <a href="/wiki/Helmeppo" title="Helmeppo">Helmeppo</a> and <a href="/wiki/Koby" title="Koby">Koby</a></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_Concepts">Early Concepts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d2/Early_Morgan.png/revision/latest?cb=20150829143045" class="image"><img alt="Early Morgan" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="154" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Early Morgan.png" data-image-key="Early_Morgan.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d2/Early_Morgan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150829143045" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d2/Early_Morgan.png/revision/latest?cb=20150829143045" class="image"><img alt="Early Morgan" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d2/Early_Morgan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150829143045" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="154" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Early Morgan.png" data-image-key="Early_Morgan.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d2/Early_Morgan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150829143045" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Early_Morgan.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">An early Morgan design, included in <a href="/wiki/Volume_1" title="Volume 1">Volume 1</a>'s bonus materials.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Eiichiro_Oda" title="Eiichiro Oda">Eiichiro Oda</a> initially tried several designs intending for Morgan to look like a "crazier" version of Helmeppo, especially in chin and hairstyle. After an editor belittled these early designs as "lame," Morgan was overhauled to look more sober and intimidating, though he still shared a number of his son's physical traits.
</p><p>Oda had originally conceived the name 'Chop' for Morgan, but claimed that he "didn't dare" to actually publish it (as "Sailor Chop"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">水兵チョップ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Suihei choppu</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> sounded identical to "Horizon Chop"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">水平チョップ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Suihei choppu</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>, the latter being a signature move of professional wrestler <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Giant_Baba" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Giant Baba">Giant Baba</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Adaptation_Differences">Adaptation Differences</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Anime_Differences">Anime Differences</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="East_Blue_Saga_2">East Blue Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6e/Morgan%27s_Shocked_Reaction.png/revision/latest?cb=20230722024556" class="image"><img alt="Morgan&#39;s Shocked Reaction" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Morgan&#39;s Shocked Reaction.png" data-image-key="Morgan%27s_Shocked_Reaction.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6e/Morgan%27s_Shocked_Reaction.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230722024556" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6e/Morgan%27s_Shocked_Reaction.png/revision/latest?cb=20230722024556" class="image"><img alt="Morgan&#39;s Shocked Reaction" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6e/Morgan%27s_Shocked_Reaction.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230722024556" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Morgan&#39;s Shocked Reaction.png" data-image-key="Morgan%27s_Shocked_Reaction.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6e/Morgan%27s_Shocked_Reaction.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230722024556" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Morgan%27s_Shocked_Reaction.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Morgan agitated at Luffy's bounty</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the manga, Morgan is shown openly maiming <a href="/wiki/Rokkaku" title="Rokkaku">Rokkaku</a> for refusing to pursue Rika, his axe-hand leaving a visible gash in Rokkaku's side. The anime somewhat censors this, omitting any visible blood and re-framing the blow to look like it came from the axe's blunt handle.
</p><p>Additionally, the anime expands Morgan's reaction at Luffy's <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi">abilities</a> into a full description of <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruits</a> (as the manga events in <a href="/wiki/Chapter_1" title="Chapter 1">Chapter 1</a> introducing Devil Fruits had been moved to <a href="/wiki/Episode_4" title="Episode 4">Episode 4</a>). Interestingly, he gives two examples—the <a href="/wiki/Mera_Mera_no_Mi" title="Mera Mera no Mi">power to breathe fire</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gura_Gura_no_Mi" title="Gura Gura no Mi">the power to raise tsunamis</a>—that inadvertently foreshadow <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Portgas D. Ace</a> and <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Edward Newgate</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Finally, the anime adds Morgan to the interlude between the <a href="/wiki/Arlong_Park_Arc" title="Arlong Park Arc">Arlong Park</a> and <a href="/wiki/Loguetown_Arc" title="Loguetown Arc">Loguetown arcs</a>, showing him inside his cell and being taunted with news of Luffy's <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>30,000,000 bounty by one of his former subordinates.<sup id="cite_ref-ep45_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ep45-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Diary_of_Koby-Meppo_2">Diary of Koby-Meppo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Morgan's post-escape attitude is somewhat expanded by the anime, where he explicitly states his intent to (re)build a "Morgan Empire". In addition, Helmeppo—with <a href="/wiki/Koby" title="Koby">Koby</a>'s help—tries to fight him instead of simply fleeing him; though Morgan easily overpowers them both, he throws them overboard instead of killing or seriously injuring them, claiming they are not worth the effort.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Live-Action_Differences">Live-Action Differences</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In the live-action series, Morgan's personality is toned down. While he is still overly prideful, as the numerous posters and statues of him around the 153rd Branch demonstrate, he is much more charismatic and not nearly as antagonistic toward his underlings; notably, the scenes of him killing a Marine for scratching his statue as well as threatening to kill anyone who fails to capture Luffy's group are omitted.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> Because of this, he remains in command of the 153rd Branch after his defeat, with his underlings having no reason to mutiny or arrest him. However, he is later arrested by Garp for lying about how Luffy's invasion of the base transpired.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Translation_and_Dub_Issues">Translation and Dub Issues</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>While Morgan's overall brutality is retained in the <a href="/wiki/4Kids_Entertainment" title="4Kids Entertainment">4Kids</a> dub (including all of his threats against <a href="/wiki/Rika" title="Rika">Rika</a>, as well as his own men), the specific dialogue is softened in many areas. For instance, his command that his men kill themselves for hesitating against <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a> and <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Zoro</a> is changed to a veiled threat for them to "shake hands" with his axe-hand.
</p><p>Like most of the anime's tobacco depictions, his cigar is digitally removed in the 4Kids dub.
</p>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Non-Playable_Appearances">Non-Playable Appearances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D33&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Grand_Battle!_2" title="Grand Battle! 2">Grand Battle! 2</a></i></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Appearances">Other Appearances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D34&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Cultural_References">Cultural References</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D35&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>In <a href="https://gintama.fandom.com/wiki/Episode_50" class="extiw" title="w:c:gintama:Episode 50">Episode 50</a> of the <a href="https://gintama.fandom.com/wiki/Gintama" class="extiw" title="w:c:gintama:Gintama"><i>Gintama</i></a> anime, a Morgan parody is "played" by <a href="https://gintama.fandom.com/wiki/Hasegawa_Taizou" class="extiw" title="w:c:gintama:Hasegawa Taizou">Hasegawa Taizou</a> in <a href="https://gintama.fandom.com/wiki/Shimura_Tae" class="extiw" title="w:c:gintama:Shimura Tae">Tae</a>'s proposal for a new show called <i>DragonBleaPiece</i>.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D36&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Morgan is the first character in the series to address Luffy by the <a href="/wiki/Epithet" title="Epithet">epithet</a> "Straw Hat".</li>
<li>Morgan's favorite food is <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Haute_cuisine" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Haute cuisine">Haute cuisine</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_4-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>In the anime, Morgan is shown to have a safe in the wall just off the floor in his office. In it, he keeps some kind of box and a map of the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Line" title="Grand Line">Grand Line</a>, which <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a> was hunted for. Having made her way into the office, she discovers a note instead of a map, which says that <a href="/wiki/Buggy" title="Buggy">Buggy</a> has already taken the map.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>In the Chinese mobile game <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_King_Battle" title="One Piece King Battle">One Piece King Battle</a>, Morgan's past as a young man is detailed. In the game, Morgan grew up with <a href="/wiki/Fullbody" title="Fullbody">Fullbody</a> and <a href="/wiki/Marine_X" title="Marine X">Marine X</a>, with whom he joined the Marines. Morgan's in-game stats were boosted when fighting alongside Marine X. Because this information is from a region-exclusive video game, it is non-canon.</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="SBS-Based_Trivia">SBS-Based Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMorgan%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D37&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>Oda has stated that he drew Morgan's name from a real-life pirate.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> This pirate is most likely <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_Morgan" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Henry Morgan">Sir Henry Morgan</a> (namesake of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Captain_Morgan" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Captain Morgan">famous rum brand</a>), who also began his career as a law-abiding sailor.</li>
<li>Oda explained in an <a href="/wiki/SBS" title="SBS">SBS</a> that had Morgan been a Marine on the Grand Line he would have held the rank of Lieutenant, as there is a three-rank difference between the Headquarters Marines and Auxiliary Marines (Marines stationed in one of the Four Blues).<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>

      <a href="/wiki/Chapter_96" title="Chapter 96">Chapter 96</a>, cover story: <a href="/wiki/Diary_of_Koby-Meppo" title="Diary of Koby-Meppo">Diary of Koby-Meppo</a> Vol. 12&#32;and <a href="/wiki/Episode_68" title="Episode 68">Episode 68</a>,&#32;Morgan (and a terrified Helmeppo) sail off in a Marine lifeboat.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-30"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-30">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text"><i>One Piece</i> Manga&#32;and Anime — <a href="/wiki/Volume_12" title="Volume 12">Vol. 12</a>
      <a href="/wiki/Chapter_106" title="Chapter 106">Chapter 106</a>, cover story: <a href="/wiki/Diary_of_Koby-Meppo" title="Diary of Koby-Meppo">Diary of Koby-Meppo</a> Vol. 20&#32;and <a href="/wiki/Episode_68" title="Episode 68">Episode 68</a>,&#32;Helmeppo, soaking wet, returns to Garp's ship and a relieved Koby.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-31"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-31">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text"><i>One Piece</i> Manga&#32;and Anime — <a href="/wiki/Volume_12" title="Volume 12">Vol. 12</a>
      <a href="/wiki/Chapter_105" title="Chapter 105">Chapter 105</a>, cover story: <a href="/wiki/Diary_of_Koby-Meppo" title="Diary of Koby-Meppo">Diary of Koby-Meppo</a> Vol. 19&#32;and <a href="/wiki/Episode_68" title="Episode 68">Episode 68</a>,&#32;Morgan, alone, continues on his way.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-32"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-32">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text"><i>One Piece</i> Manga — <a href="/wiki/Volume_1" title="Volume 1">Vol. 1</a>&#32;(p. 124),&#32;Between <a href="/wiki/Chapter_5" title="Chapter 5">Chapters 5</a> and <a href="/wiki/Chapter_6" title="Chapter 6">6</a>, in a sort of precursor to the <a href="/wiki/SBS" title="SBS">SBS</a>, Oda explains the creation of Morgan and Helmeppo, including concept art.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-33"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-33">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text"><i>One Piece</i> Anime — <a href="/wiki/Episode_3" title="Episode 3">Episode 3</a>,&#32;Morgan speaks about Devil Fruit users that can breathe fire and create tsunamis, years before Ace and Whitebeard were even implied in the manga, let alone demonstrated their abilities.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-34"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-34">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text"><i>One Piece</i> Anime — <a href="/wiki/Episode_68" title="Episode 68">Episode 68</a>,&#32;For the first time, <a href="/wiki/Helmeppo" title="Helmeppo">Helmeppo</a> takes his Marine enlistment seriously, and declares Morgan will be the first outlaw he arrests.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-35"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-35">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text"><i>One Piece</i> Live-Action — <a href="/wiki/Romance_Dawn_(Live-Action)" title="Romance Dawn (Live-Action)">Romance Dawn</a>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-36"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-36">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text"><i>One Piece</i> Live-Action — <a href="/wiki/The_Man_in_the_Straw_Hat" title="The Man in the Straw Hat">The Man in the Straw Hat</a>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-37"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-37">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text"><i>One Piece</i> Anime — <a href="/wiki/Episode_3" title="Episode 3">Episode 3</a>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-38"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-38">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/SBS" title="SBS">SBS</a> <i>One Piece</i> Manga — <a href="/wiki/SBS_Volume_4" title="SBS Volume 4">Vol. 4</a>&#32;(p. 48),&#32;Oda states that Morgan's name comes from a real pirate.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-39"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-39">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/SBS" title="SBS">SBS</a> <i>One Piece</i> Manga — <a href="/wiki/SBS_Volume_29" title="SBS Volume 29">Vol. 29</a>&#32;(p. 26),&#32;Oda explains the difference between the captains at Marine bases and those at the Marine Headquarters.</span>
